Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Refer to the instructions for simple patching of the code

<br>

<span class="line"><!---->2. Start chromium in chromeos<!----></span>



<br>





3. open chrome://crostini-upgrader and click Upgrade, then close chrome://crostini-upgrader.



<span class="line"><!---->3. open chrome://crostini-upgrader and click Upgrade, then close chrome://crostini-upgrader.<!----></span>

What went wrong?



<span class="line"><!---->What went wrong?<!----></span>

# Use-after-Free on crostini::CrostiniExportImport::OpenFileDialog



<span class="line"><!----># Use-after-Free on crostini::CrostiniExportImport::OpenFileDialog<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





## Root Cause and some notes



<span class="line"><!---->## Root Cause and some notes<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[0] The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence



<span class="line"><!---->[0] The `web_contents` is posted to a separate sequence<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time the it runs, causing a UAF in OnBackupPathChecked(finial in OpenFileDialog) callback.



<span class="line"><!---->[1] `web_contents` may be destroyed in UI by the time the it runs, causing a UAF in OnBackupPathChecked(finial in OpenFileDialog) callback.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The pattern of this vulnerability is similar to this issue.



<span class="line"><!---->The pattern of this vulnerability is similar to this issue.<!----></span>



<br>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233975



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233975"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1233975<!----></a>



<br>

[2] The root cause of this vulnerability is very clear, but to quick trigger this vulnerability, we need to patch some codes.

1. First add sleep(10) at the beginning of the base::PathExists function.



<span class="line"><!---->1. First add sleep(10) at the beginning of the base::PathExists function.<!----></span>



<br>





Since this is a base function, in order not to cause side effects, I added a Test function with a flag



<span class="line"><!---->Since this is a base function, in order not to cause side effects, I added a Test function with a flag<!----></span>

other:



<span class="line"><!---->other:<!----></span>



<br>





Because CrostiniUpgrader is KeyedService, It will only be free after ChromeOS is closed.



<span class="line"><!---->Because CrostiniUpgrader is KeyedService, It will only be free after ChromeOS is closed.<!----></span>



<br>





So even if the webcontent is free, the OnBackupPathChecked callback will still happen.



<span class="line"><!---->So even if the webcontent is free, the OnBackupPathChecked callback will still happen.<!----></span>

Since backup can be called directly through the mojo interface [0], a compromised renderer may trigger the UAF without interaction(maybe?).



<span class="line"><!---->Since backup can be called directly through the mojo interface [0], a compromised renderer may trigger the UAF without interaction(maybe?).<!----></span>



<br>

  // user will be shown a dialog to decide where to store the backup.

<br>





  Backup(bool show_file_chooser);



<span class="line"><!---->  Backup(bool show_file_chooser);<!----></span>

crostini_upgrader: Handle content::WebContents through weak pointers



<span class="line"><!---->crostini_upgrader: Handle content::WebContents through weak pointers<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





content::WebContents is not owned by the upgrader but gets passed to



<span class="line"><!---->content::WebContents is not owned by the upgrader but gets passed to<!----></span>



<br>





callbacks, so we need to be able to check if it has been destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->callbacks, so we need to be able to check if it has been destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Please answer the following questions so that we can safely process your merge request:



<span class="line"><!---->Please answer the following questions so that we can safely process your merge request:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Why does your merge fit within the merge criteria for these milestones?



<span class="line"><!---->1. Why does your merge fit within the merge criteria for these milestones?<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome Browser: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome Browser: <!----></span>





https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/branches



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/branches"><!---->https://chromiumdash.appspot.com/branches<!----></a>



<br>





- Chrome OS: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome OS: <!----></span>

<br>





2. What changes specifically would you like to merge? Please link to Gerrit.



<span class="line"><!---->2. What changes specifically would you like to merge? Please link to Gerrit.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Have the changes been released and tested on canary?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Have the changes been released and tested on canary?<!----></span>



<br>





4. Is this a new feature? If yes, is it behind a Finch flag and are experiments active in any release channels?



<span class="line"><!---->4. Is this a new feature? If yes, is it behind a Finch flag and are experiments active in any release channels?<!----></span>



<br>





5. [Chrome OS only]: Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? 



<span class="line"><!---->5. [Chrome OS only]: Was the change reviewed and approved by the Eng Prod Representative? <!----></span>





https://goto.google.com/cros-engprodcomponents



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://goto.google.com/cros-engprodcomponents"><!---->https://goto.google.com/cros-engprodcomponents<!----></a>



<br>





6. If this merge addresses a major issue in the stable channel, does it require manual verification by the test team? If so, please describe required testing.



<span class="line"><!---->6. If this merge addresses a major issue in the stable channel, does it require manual verification by the test team? If so, please describe required testing.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
